```mermaid
sequenceDiagram

    participant MSW
    participant handleShipmentEtaVINs
    participant getScenario

    end
    handleShipmentEtaVINs-->>MSW: res(ctx.json(responseBody))
    MSW-->>Client: JSON response with VIN data
```

flowchart TD
    A[API Request] --> B{Endpoint Type}

    C --> E[getScenario]
    D --> F[getScenario]
    E --> G{scenario check}
    F --> H{scenario check}
    G -->|largeTotalCount| I[Set total_shipments = 1000000]
    G -->|other| J[Use default data]
    H -->|largeTotalCount| K[Set total_shipments = 1000000]
    H -->|other| L[Use default data]
    I --> M[Return shipment ETA response]
    J --> M
    K --> N[Return VIN response]
    L --> N

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ShipmentEtaResponse {
        +Object meta
        +Array data
        +Number total_shipments
    }
    class Meta {
        +Number totalPages
        +Number currentPage
        +Number totalCount
    }
    class ShipmentEtaData {
        +String shipmentStatusCreatedDateUTC
        +String shipmentStatusActualEventDateUTC
        +String etaCalculationShipmentStatusCode
        +String etaCalculationPointOfInterest
        +String etaCalculationLatitude
        +String etaCalculationLongitude
        +String etaCalculationCity
        +String etaCalculationStateOrProvince
        +String etaCalculationCountry
        +String etaUTC
        +String etaModelName
        +String numberOfDaysInHistory
        +String percentileUsedInCalculation
        +String etaModelVersion
        +String etaModelKey
        +Number numberOfObservationsInModel
        +String shipmentActualArrivalTime
        +String shipmentUltimateDestinationCode
        +String shipmentUltimateDestinationName
        +String etaDestinationTime
        +Number etaDifference
        +String triggerType
        +String triggerMode
        +String triggerLocationName
        +String etaAlgorithm
        +String lifeCycleState
    }
    class VINResponse {
        +Object meta
        +Array data
        +Number total_shipments
    }
    class VINData {
        +String id
    }
    ShipmentEtaResponse --> Meta
    ShipmentEtaResponse --> ShipmentEtaData
    VINResponse --> Meta
    VINResponse --> VINData
```
